<Review>If it weren't for all the great experiences I've had here and the quick customer service I almost always get, I'd leave a one star review. However, my most recent experience was so abysmal that I felt obligated to leave this review.

Two nights ago on December 10th, I made an order for a pepperoni mushroom pizza and a caesar salad at around 5pm. I arrived at 5:38 when my pizza was said to be ready. I sat in my car outside the restaurant as I was expecting a carside delivery. Over the course of the next two hours I watched many people come and go, the vast majority shuffling back to their car empty handed. I called the store at 5:50, and was told that my order would be ready shortly. I waited in my car for another hour, and during that period, every single person who had gotten there before me, and almost every single person who'd gotten there after me had left with no pizza.

At 6:50, I made another phone call, not to complain, but just to see what was going on, and got no answer. I decided to walk in after another 40 minutes just to get some sort of update. After the two people in front of me lost patience over their order and left, I waited until I was able to speak to someone. The staff were reluctant to talk to me, which I understand as I saw a couple people in front of me chew them out, which kind of sucked because I don't think any of them had anticipated that night. The phones were ringing, and going unanswered because the few workers who were there were scrambling to get every last pizza out, so there wasn't all that much time for human interaction. I eventually got to talk to one of the employees and they mentioned they were short staffed that night. It made sense, as it looked like there were less than 10 people there.

I finally received my pizza after a whopping 2 hour wait. I mentioned that it came with a caesar salad, which was promptly brought to me. I brought my order home and came to realize two things: one, that it was the worst pizza I'd ever had, and two, that the caesar salad was expired, only by a day though, so I still ate it. The crust was way too thick and mushy, the cheese looked like it had been sitting there for way too long, the topping distribution looked way too rushed and uneven, the pizza was barely sliced, and the whole pizza was basically room temperature.

I can't blame the employees for this, as it seemed like they were all working hard that night and figuring out how to manage the situation. Nobody was happy that night, and many customers walked out empty handed. I just want to know what was going on that night.

I could have literally driven to the domino's in Venice, driven back to Whittier, and gotten my pizza faster than I got it here.<//Review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMTwXZCr5SaM2yW_cw0thr7HnARiSSgkoSbrn3X=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures>< Resp>

They get orders wrong, even when ordering from the app. If you are part of the domino's rewards program, they questioned the free pizza you earned, "just to make sure that it is really free". I miss the Beverly/Norwalk location. They were good at what they did. This location is just problem after problem. They need better training, supervision and signage. < review>
This is really quality Ethiopian food, so I partially understand all the hype. However, they really need to adjust their prices for take-out. You are paying for high-end luxury fine-dining, but to-go in a styrofoam container. It's just simply not worth it. You can get similar quality take-out Ethiopian food elsewhere for half the price. When indoor dining returns, I'm sure this is a fine spot for a pleasant evening out. (I do have to congratulate them for their incredibly safe contact-free takeout system).</review>

< Review>
Meals by Genet is one of my favorites, if not my favorite place. The food is always so good. The servers are very nice. I highly recommend this place for locals in the neighborhood and also for people visiting from out of town. The food is always consistently very good. I really enjoy taking my out of town guests there to dine. They always enjoy the food and the experience at Meals by Genet. For those unfamiliar to Ethiopian food, the style of dining is communal. A great choice for families and children at age ten really like it also. That is really nice because children at that age can be a little picky about their food. Meals by Genet is a great place.every time we go. We are always welcomed with smiling faces. On every visit we always order two veggie platters. One is never enough.< /Review>

Delicious food for vegetarians and meat eaters alike. Good lighting and ambiance to take a date. There is limited seating so it is worth getting reservations. Luckily someone cancelled and they let us in. We had honey wine and Ethiopian beer which were both great, and one order of tofu tibs and a veggie combo. <name>Paul Smith<//name><date>1477193901075<//date>< Rate>
4<//Rate>
< review>
This was our second trip to this intimate little Ethiopian restaurant, and although the first visit was almost a year ago, the food has been consistently delicious.

The restaurant is sparsely decorated, so it can get quite loud with everyone's conversations bouncing off the walls - although never deafening.

I'd recommend making a booking, because the small restaurant can fill up pretty quickly, especially if a couple of groups are eating.

Staff have always been friendly and attentive, but make sure you listen carefully to their description of the meal, especially if you can't tolerate spicy food.

If you pick a few 'proteins' to go with the 'vegetarian combination', the meal can get reasonably expensive rather quickly. I wish they did half serves!

There's limited parking in the back lane - if you arrive early enough!

A great place to have something a bit different from the burger and burrito staples of LA.</review>

A lot off guarenteed Produce including unusual fruits. Cold waters and some single beers and small batch brewers.  Peets' coffee a dentist a pet store where you can wash you small or large doggie. Or cat!

Two hair cutters for guys including great clips.
Salon including tanning(?). Not safe for folks did eptable to u v rays overexposure according to the FDA AND the National Safety Council and IHHS. Karate school, BBQ. Sushi, organic yogurt(frozen), Asian specialty and several dentists and even a massage place that is not shady. Expensive membership though, in most opinionated.  Banks, apartment community that was built by Shea over  decade ago almost two.
It is truly an integral part of the shopped and across from a mediterrian and Mexican style cafe and optometrist.  Some qualitative and some quantitative items/businesses. Here is a lot of one stop shopping and a large city water park and city park behind in Emerald Glen.
If living or coming from Tracy worth a stop. Miles from fuel stop though. Across freeway is a it's and a Shell. Waterford is busy even with an CSAA/AAA branch office too. Decent place.</review>
